  ut ti\'ShTha brahmaNas pate deva\`yanta\'s tvemahe  |\\
  upa\` pra ya\'ntu ma\`rutaH\' su\`daana\'va\` indra\' praa\`shuur bha\'vaa\` sacaa\'  || \EN{1}{040}{01} \\
  tvaam id dhi sa\'hasas putra\` martya\' upabruu\`te dhane\' hi\`te  |\\
  su\`viirya\'m maruta\` aa svashvyaM\` dadhii\'ta\` yo va\' aaca\`ke  || \EN{1}{040}{02} \\
  praitu\` brahma\'Na\`s patiH\` pra de\`vy etu suu\`nR^itaa\'  |\\
  acChaa\' vii\`raM narya\'m pa\`~Nktiraa\'dhasaM de\`vaa ya\`j~naM na\'yantu naH  || \EN{1}{040}{03} \\
  yo vaa\`ghate\` dadaa\'ti suu\`naraM\` vasu\` sa dha\'tte\` akShi\'ti\` shravaH\'  |\\
  tasmaa\` iLaaM\' su\`viiraa\`m aa ya\'jaamahe su\`pratuu\'rtim ane\`hasa\'m  || \EN{1}{040}{04} \\
  pra nuu\`nam brahma\'Na\`s pati\`r mantraM\' vadaty u\`kthyam  |\\
  yasmi\`nn indro\` varu\'No mi\`tro a\'rya\`maa de\`vaa okaaM\'si cakri\`re  || \EN{1}{040}{05} \\
  tam id vo\'cemaa vi\`dathe\'Shu sha\`mbhuva\`m mantraM\' devaa ane\`hasa\'m  |\\
  i\`maaM ca\` vaaca\'m prati\`harya\'thaa naro\` vishved vaa\`maa vo\' ashnavat  || \EN{1}{040}{06} \\
  ko de\'va\`yanta\'m ashnava\`j janaM\` ko vR^i\`ktaba\'rhiSham  |\\
  pra\-pra\' daa\`shvaan pa\`styaabhir asthitaanta\`rvaava\`t kShayaM\' dadhe  || \EN{1}{040}{07} \\
  upa\' kSha\`tram pR^i\'~ncii\`ta hanti\` raaja\'bhir bha\`ye ci\'t sukShi\`tiM da\'dhe  |\\
  naasya\' va\`rtaa na ta\'ru\`taa ma\'haadha\`ne naarbhe\' asti va\`jriNaH\'  || \EN{1}{040}{08} \\

  yaM rakSha\'nti\` prace\'taso\` varu\'No mi\`tro a\'rya\`maa  |\\

  yam baa\`hute\'va\` pipra\'ti\` paanti\` martyaM\' ri\`ShaH  |\\

  sam puu\'Sha\`nn adhva\'nas tira\` vy aMho\' vimuco napaat  |\\

  agne\` viva\'svad u\`Shasa\'sh ci\`traM raadho\' amartya  |\\
